 On the 136th anniversary of the narrator Munshi Premchand, Google India remembered him in a unique way
 sabase bade search ingine ne apane home pej par premchand ke prasiddh upanyaas 'godaan' kaa doodle lagaaya he
 Born in Lamhi village of Uttar Pradesh in the year 1880, Premchand's name is taken with great respect in the Hindi literature world
 unke upanyaas or kahani desh hi nahin duniyabar main pasand kiye jate hai
 The specialty of the literature written by him is that his characters and their problems are relevant even today
 unke upanyaas 'godaan', 'nirmala', 'gaban', 'seva sadan' bhartiya samaaj ke taane-bane, gramin janajivan or kisaanon kii vyathaa ko dikhaate hai
 Her stories are 'poose Ki Raat', 'bade Ghar Ki Beti', 'chess Players' classics
 premchand ko 'kalam kaa sipaahi' bhi kaha jaataa he
 The comments premchand kii zyaadaatar kahaniyaan ek acchhee sikh ke saath khatm hoti hai
 Whether the story of young child Hamid is 'idgah' or 'panch Parmeshwar', which gives the message of social justice
 premchand kaa asli naam dhanpat raay tha, aath saal kii umr main unki maa kaa dehanth ho gaya or unke pita duusari shaadi kar lee
 Premchand was married at the age of 15, after the death of his father in 1897, he was given the responsibility of the whole family at the age of 17
 kuch samay baad unki patni unhen chhodkar maayke chali gai
 Premchand later married child widow Shivrani Devi, from whom he had three children
 saal 1880 main uttar pradesh ke lamahi gaanv main janmen premchand kaa naam hindi sahitya jagat main behad sammaan ke saath liya jaataa he
 His novels and stories are not only liked around the world
 unke dwaara likhe sahitya kii khaasiyat he ki unke kirdaar or unki samasyaayein aaj bhi praasangik hai
 His novels 'godan', 'nirmala', 'embezzlement', 'seva Sadan' show the fabric of Indian society, rural life and the agony of farmers
 unki kahaniyaan 'pus kii raat', 'bade ghar kii beti', 'shatranj ke khilaadi' kaaljayi rachanaaen hai
 Premchand is also known as 'the soldier of the pen'
 tippaniyan Most of Premchand's stories end with a good lesson

 Viren Dangwal's way of seeing and identifying reality in poetry has been very different, unique and basic
 san 1991 main prakashit unka pehla kavita-sangrah 'isi duniya main' agar aaj ek dashak baad bhi utana hi praasangik or mahatvapurn lagata he, to isliye ki viren kii kavita ne samaaj ke saadhaaranjanon or hashiyon par sthit jivan ke jo vilakshan byore or drishy hamen diye hai, ve kavita main or kavita se baahar bhi sabase adhik baichaiyn karne vaale drishy hai
 Through poetry, Viren created a discussion of the world of many things and appearances that were often lost and unseen
 unki kavita main janavaadee parivartan kii mul pratigya thi or uski bunaavat main theth desi kism ke, khaas or aam, tatsam or tadbhav, clasik or deshaj anubhavon kii sanshlishtataa thi
 Viren Dangwal was born on 5 August 1947 in Kirtinagar, Tehri Garhwal
 unhone shuruaati shiksha mujffarnagar, saharanpur, kanpur, bareli, nainital grahan kii or ucch shiksha ke liye elahabaad vishvavidhyalay chale gaye

 saal 1971 main viren dangwaal bareli college main adhyaapan karne chale aaye
 He did journalism in Hindi and English as well as teaching
 kai akhabaaron ke liye stambh-lekhan kiya or ek hindi akhbaar ke sampadakeey salaahkaar bhi rahe
 In the meantime, he has gained considerable popularity with the collection of poetry in this world, Sastha in the vicious cycle, ink rhythm
 unke dwaara turki ke mahakavi nazim hikmat kii kavitaaon ke anuwaad pahal pustika ke rup main chape
 He translated some of the tribal folk poems in addition to the poems of Pablo Neruda, Bertolt Brecht, Vasco Popa, Miroslav Holub, Tadeusha Roosevich etc
, very important names in the field of world poetry
 dangwaal kii kai kavitaaon ke anuwaad bangla, marathi, punjabi, malayalam or angrezi main prakashit hue hai
 Dangwal has been awarded the Raghuveer Sahay Smriti Award, Shrikant Verma Smriti Award, Shamsher Samman and Sahitya Akademi Award for his poet's work
 viren dangwaal kii vilakshan kavy-drushti parjanya, vanya, varun, dyos jaise vaidic pratikon or oont, hathi, gaay, makkhi, samose, papite, imali jaisi ati loukik vastuon kii ek saath shinaakht karti hui apane samay main ek jaruri hastkshep karti thi
 The irony, satire, farce and realization of a human absurdity have been well-known elements of Viren's poetry and combined with a deep political commitment, he becomes the voice of the marginalized human being
 unki kavitaaon main kavyayuktiyon kaa aisa vistaar he, jo ghar or baahar, nijee or saarvajanik, aantarik or bahya ko ek saath sametataa hua zyaada buniyadi kavyarthon ko sambhav karata he
 The things called bizarre, strange, infirm, suppressed and misguided, interconnected here, spur a spontaneous debate with power, power and nobility, and we find how great conflict and great beauty are hidden in small things
 saadhaaran logon, jeev-jantuon or vastuon se bani manushyata kaa gungan or yathasthiti main parivartan kii gahari ummid viren dangwaal kii kavitaaon kaa mukhya swar he
 It is a thrilling experience to see and feel the expansion of this voice, the experiences stirring in it
 viren dangwaal se pehle shaayad hindi kavita main itane anuraag ke saath kabhi nahin aaye hai

 unhone kaha ki grahamantri ne jo faisla liya he, ham sab uske saath hai or kashmir main sijafire jari rahegaa
 Shelling in Arnia: Pakistani Rangers have been firing from mortar since late night on Monday in Arnia sector of Jammu
 seemaa se satee kareeb teen bhartiya chaukiyon ko nishaanaa banaaya gaya he
 In the Ramgarh sector also, before firing, the Pakistani troops targeted the BSF advance posts with small arms and mortar in the night in Narayanpur area of ramgarh sector of Samba district
 haalanki, iske kuch ghante pehle usne biguef se golibari rokane kii apil kii thi kyonki biguef kii karrwai main seemaa paar ek jawan kii maut ho gai thi
 The BSF also released a 19-second thermal imagery footage in which a Pakistani outpost is seen collapsing in India's response after being fired from that side of the border without provocation
 bataa den ki antarrashtriya seemaa par pakistan kii ore se 15 may se ab tak bina kisi uksaave ke hui golibari main biguef ke do jawan shahid ho chuke hai
 Apart from this, four people were killed and 11 others were injured in the firing on Friday in Jammu
 seemaa paar se golibari or golabari kii 700 se adhik ghatnaon main is saal 18 suraksha karmiyon sahit 38 log maare gaye hai or kai ghayal hue hai
 The film 'main Tera Hero' was not a hit that the planning of the sequel of this film has started
 jaahir he sikval he to varun to film main honge hi
 But there is a slight change in Part 2
 wo yah ki is baar main role main varun kii jagah sonakshi hongi
 That is, Sonakshi Sinha will be the protagonist of the story
 film 'main tera hero' main do hiroinon ke saath varun dhawan ne romance kiya
 Similarly, in the film Main Teri Heroine, Sonakshi Madam will be seen flirting with two boys
 film ke hero honge arjuna kapur or varun dhawan
 Sonakshi Sinha, Arjun Kapoor and Varun Dhawan all three have inherited acting
 teenon ek duusare ko bachapan se jaanate hai
 Sonakshi's film Tevar with Arjun Kapoor is going to be released soon
 vahiin varun dhawan ke saath sonakshi sinha ne ek fishan megsine ke liye modelling kii thi
 Now these three are going to appear on screen together
 haalanki is film kaa produsar or diarector koun hoga, ye ab tak saaf nahin ho paaya he
 Actually, these three Bollywood stars were present at the success party of the film 'main Tera Hero'
 party kii ek tasviir fasebuk par post karte hue sonakshi ne likhaa- 'main tera hero part2- main teri heroin
 'that is, if by now the idea of a sequel may not have come in the mind of Ekta Kapoor and David Dhawan, then this Facebook post of Sonakshi Madam will definitely light up their mind
 bhartiya relon main toilet lagane kii baat lagbhag sau saal puranihai
 But you will be surprised to know that fifty years after the first train in India felt the need for toilet
 lekin yah khyaal british hukumat ko ek karaara patr milaneke baad aayaa
 This letter was written by a traveler in 1909
 aaie jaanate hai aisa kya tha us patr main?1909menokhil chandra sen naamak ek yatri paisanger train se yatra kar rahe the
 He wrote a letter to the Sahibganj Rail Division's office about the experiences that occurred during that time
 patr kuch yun tha-"priyashreeman,main paisager train se ahmadpur stesan aayaa or meraa petdard kii vajah se sooj rahaa tha
 i went there alone to defecate
 main vahaan nivrittaho hi rahaa tha ki guard ne siti bajaanaa shuru kar diya, train chhootane vaali thi
 i ran a lota in one hand and a dhoti in the other hand and then fell on the platform
 meri dhoti khul gai or mujhe vahaan maujuud sabhi mahila-purushon ke saamne sharminda honapada
 i missed the train and i stayed at Ahmedpur station
 yah kitni buree baat he ki ek yatri shouch ke liye gaya ho aurtrain kaa guard kuch minute uskaa intjaar bhi nahin kar saktaa
 i humbly request you to pay a heavy fine on that guard for the betterment of the public
 nahin to main is prakaran kisuchana samachar patron ko de duungaa
 Your trusted servantokhil Chandra Sen

 ) Attacking the Lieutenant Governor indirectly, he said that the 'elected' people should be above the 'selected' people, who are not (elected) public representatives
 saath hi kaha ki loktantr main janata ko chaynit logon se upar hona chahie

 ) Saina Nehwal has 80191 points in the latest badminton world rankings
 duusare number par spain kii carolina marin hai 79578 ankon ke saath or tisare number par china kii lee zuerei hai 72964 ankon ke saath
 Saina Nehwal is obviously very happy while training at Prakash Padukone Badminton Academy in Bangalore
 wo maanati hai ki unki kismat acchhee he ki wo jaldi hi dubaara number 1 khilaadi ban gai hai
 She does not get tired of thanking her coach Vimal Kumar for all this
 wo kahati hai ki pichley saat maheene vimal kumaar ne unke saath kadi mehnat kii he or in sabakaa nateeja he ki wo phir se world number 1 ban gai hai
 Two superstars of a city
 
 
 do aise khilaadi jinka dabadabaa bharat hi nahin puri duniya main he
 Two World No
1 players in the world and both from Hyderabad
 donon ke khel alag hai, maidan alag par apane-apane court par karname karti in donon world champion main bahut si baaten ek jaisi hai
 Both are on the spotlight on many magazines today
 praayojak companiyaan, fans or jaankaar inpar karodon kaa daanv lagane ko taiyaar hai
 But before reaching this destination, both of them had to cross a mountain of difficulties
 sina nehwal kahati hai ki baat hyderabad kii nahin he
 The matter is about India
 acchhee baat ye he ki ab kai or yuva khilaadiyon ke liye world number 1 bananaa gairmumkin nahin lagegaa
 Sania is also giving a similar response
 wo kahati hai ki ye kamaal kaa ittifaaq he ki donon world number 1 khilaadi ek hi shahar se hai
 But it is a matter of pride for the whole country and now many young players can see the dream of becoming World No
1
 sania mirza ne qareeb do saal pehle singles khelnaa chhodane kaa faisalaa kiya or dubles main world number 1 banane kaa khwab paalane lageen
 Meanwhile, in women's doubles, she also had to change partner
 lekin sania ne bulandi par pahunchakar hi dam liya
 The story of Saina is also similar
 sania kii tarah hi sina bhi lakhon yuvaaon ke liye role model hai
 Saina has been in the top ten continuously for the last five years, breaking the difficult wall of China and then reached where many players of the world have pledged to reach
 tippaniyan The joy of both becoming World No
1 can be felt on the common roads, schools and grounds of Hyderabad
 kai yuva khilaadiyon ko is baat kaa ahsaas he ki in donon khilaadiyon ko top par pahunchane ke liye kya kuch karnaa padaa hoga
 Olympic medalist Saina Nehwal and three Grand Slam winners Sania Mirza of mixed doubles have also gone through a period of controversy
 lekin har chunauti ko chota sabit karti huin in khilaadiyon ne naa sirf hyderabad balki bhartiya khelon kaa naam duniya bhar main roshan kar diya he

 baat india kii he

1
 sania bhi kuch aisi hi pratikriya de rahi hai

1 in doubles
 is bich mahila dubles main unhen partner badalane kii zarurat bhi padi

 sina kii kahani bhi kuch aisi hi he
